Current Status of Silver Circulation 42

(New York) In the week ending July 19th, US silver imports totaled $7,281,000, a decrease of $1,056,000 from the previous week. Mexico supplied the most silver, valued at $3,053,000, followed by the United Kingdom, valued at $2,670,000. Other suppliers included Peru ($209,000), Chile ($159,000), Canada ($122,000), Soviet Russia ($54,000), Mozambique ($6,000), and Guatemala ($5,000). (26th Reuters Telegram)

(London) In the week ending July 24th, the inflow and outflow of silver in the UK increased compared to the previous week. Total exports were valued at £782,000, all purchased by the United States. Total exports for the previous week were valued at £765,000, with the United States purchasing £735,000 and other countries purchasing the remaining £30,000. Silver imports into the UK this week were valued at £736,000, with Japan accounting for £318,000, Soviet Russia accounting for £35,000, Hong Kong accounting for £269,000, the Netherlands accounting for £48,000, and India accounting for £22,000. The total imports for the previous week were £590,000. Net exports this week were £46,000, while net exports for the previous week were £175,000. (27th Reuters Telegram)

The Mysterious Lake Baikal 43

(TASS, July 4, Ulan-Ude dispatch) The mystery of Lake Baikal has attracted the attention of scientists around the world. The lakebed contains vast amounts of fish, forests, and minerals. The Baikal Basin is the largest basin in the world, surrounded by mountains. The highest of these mountains rises 1,400 meters above the lake surface and 1,850 meters above sea level. The lake is 660 kilometers long, 85 kilometers wide, and approximately 2,200 kilometers in circumference. Its area is second only to the Caspian Sea.

The deepest part of Lake Baikal, as far as is known, reaches 1,741 meters, making it the deepest freshwater lake in the world. There are 27 islands in the lake, the largest of which is Olkhon Island, which is 10 kilometers wide and 69 kilometers long. Three hundred and thirty-six rivers flow into the lake, the largest of which is the Selenga River, which is navigable. Only one river flows out of the lake, the Lower Angara River.

The lake is famous for its extremely low salt content. The lake water is clear, and white objects can be seen at a depth of 40 meters in some places. Lake Baikal has a great impact on the climate in the vicinity, regulating temperature changes. The lake water freezes completely at the end of December and melts at the end of May.

The flora and fauna at the bottom of the lake have enormous scientific value in addition to their practical benefits. As far as is known, there are 1,300 species of animals and plants, of which about 80% are local to the lake. Some carp live in water 1,500 meters deep, where the pressure reaches 150 atmospheres. Among the industrial fish, the native salmon called "Omul" ranks first, followed by sturgeon and whitefish. Among the marine animals, the native seal has special economic value, and more than 6,000 seals are caught each year.

The Baikal Basin is rich in minerals, including gold, coal, petroleum, iron, and other metals.

From a scientific point of view, Lake Baikal is a museum of ancient life that can help us solve a number of biological and geological problems. From an economic point of view, the lake provides a rich basis for the economic development of the Buryat-Mongol Autonomous Soviet Socialist Republic.

League of Nations Scheduled to Meet; France Striving to Avoid Rupture, Working to Promote Mediation; Decision on Whether Italy Will Send a Representative Undecided 44

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations decided to meet at 5:00 PM on July 31st to discuss the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. There has been no definite reply as to whether Italy will send a representative. (27th Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) People here now believe that Italy will not send a representative to the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations if it involves issues other than the border conflict. The Italian authorities are currently awaiting a reply from the Abyssinian government on this matter, but it is reported that the Italian government reserves the right to submit a statement, whether or not a representative attends. (27th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) There is now a slightly more optimistic outlook here regarding the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations to discuss the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. It is expected that the Council will put pressure on Abyssinia to agree to continue the mediation process and will also elect a fifth arbitrator. If Abyssinia agrees, the Council will reaffirm the provision in Article 5 of the 1928 Italo-Abyssinian Treaty that both parties agree not to resort to force. The Council meeting may then conclude within 48 hours. If Abyssinia insists on a comprehensive discussion and the proposal to send neutral observers to the scene, a serious situation may arise. (27th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) After Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval met with British Ambassador to France Sir Eric Phipps this morning, there has been no progress in peacefully resolving the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, but diplomatic sources believe that after convening a meeting, the Council of the League of Nations may announce a postponement of the meeting until September, so that the Italo-Abyssinian Mixed Arbitration Committee can first resume work and conduct conciliation proceedings, and the countries concerned can also take the opportunity to establish a compromise plan. If Italy accepts the appointment of a fifth neutral arbitrator designated by the Council when the Council meets, this solution will certainly be easier to initiate. (26th Havas Telegram)

(Paris) Although the Italo-Abyssinian situation is very tense, those close to Prime Minister Laval seem to hope that the Council of the League of Nations will be able to avoid a serious conflict at its meeting and postpone the issue until the end of August for further discussion, so as to allow time for diplomatic negotiations. According to general observations, the Council meeting will focus on discussing future steps. Abyssinia is asking the League of Nations to handle the whole problem, which is aided by England, while Italy insists on limiting the discussion to certain specific issues. The French political community still believes that Laval's diplomatic skills will be able to eliminate this difficulty invisibly, and it is reported that Eden will make a brief stop in Paris when he goes to Geneva, at which time Laval and Eden will be able to agree on joint action. (27th National Telegram)

Italy Ready to Resume Mediation with League of Nations 45

(London) Italy has recently received a notification from the Secretariat of the League of Nations inviting it to attend the meeting of the Council of Administration. It is now planning to send Mr. Aloisi, the Chief Secretary of the Prime Minister's Office, as the Italian representative to Geneva. It is believed here that Italy's preparation to attend the Council of Administration is not so much a new compromise towards Abyssinia as it is a gesture of friendship towards France. According to diplomatic sources, Aloisi's instructions are limited to discussing the Walwal incident. The border issue between Italian East Africa and Abyssinia, as well as the entire dispute between Italy and Abyssinia, are not included. Therefore, the initial difficulty for the Council of Administration lies in deciding whether the scope of discussion should be limited to the Walwal incident according to Italy's view, or whether a comprehensive study of the Italy-Abyssinia dispute should be conducted according to Britain's view. It is generally believed that after the anti-British demonstrations held in Rome last night, Britain's position is even less likely to change. (Havas, 26th)

(Rome) The Italian government has recently sent a memorandum to the Secretariat of the League of Nations, stating that the Italian government informed the Abyssinian government on July 4th of its willingness to resume the work of the Mixed Arbitration Commission, but the issues discussed by the Commission should be limited to the Walwal conflict. Currently, the Abyssinian government has not yet responded to Italy's notification. Therefore, the Italian government cannot immediately respond to the invitation to attend the meeting of the Council of Administration of the League of Nations. If Abyssinia accepts Italy's proposal and resumes the work of the Arbitration Commission, Italy is willing to participate in the meeting of the Council of Administration. However, what the Council of Administration discusses at that time should be limited to facilitating the work of the Arbitration Commission. If some member states of the League of Nations seek to raise other issues, Italy will reserve its attitude. (Havas, 27th)

Abyssinian Emperor Issues Declaration Seeking Peace 46

The Abyssinian Emperor in the capital, Addis Ababa, recently issued a declaration to the press, pointing out two points: (1) The Abyssinian government is determined to seek a peaceful resolution to the Italy-Abyssinia dispute. (2) The main reason for the conflict between Italy and Abyssinia is due to the different interpretations by the two governments of the treaty signed on May 16, 1908, regarding the demarcation of the border between Abyssinia and Italian Somaliland. As for the present, although Italy has accepted the submission to arbitration in principle, in fact, it is using various means to make arbitration impossible. Italy denies that the Arbitration Commission has the right to interpret which side the Walwal territory belongs to, whether the occupation of the Walwal area is legal, and refuses to appoint a fifth neutral arbitrator by the Council of Administration of the League of Nations. If so, how can the arbitration process proceed? In short, which member state of the League of Nations is openly infringing upon the sovereignty and independence of other countries, and which country is using force as a political tool for external expansion? These two should now be decided by the Council of Administration of the League of Nations. We now await the decision of the Council of Administration with great confidence. (Havas, 27th)

Today in Addis Ababa, the Abyssinian Emperor told guests that it is unfair for Britain and other countries to ban the export of arms to Abyssinia. It is even more regrettable that foreign companies undertaking contracts for military equipment needed by the Abyssinian army have suddenly terminated their contracts. The Emperor also described the organization of the Abyssinian army's combat, saying that seven main leaders each lead a corps. Although they have some independent rights for special missions, they will act jointly. Because Abyssinia's military equipment is inferior, each corps cannot adopt modern military systems, but each regiment will have countless reconnaissance teams to assist. These people are born warriors and act quickly. The most difficult thing for Abyssinia is the shortage of ammunition. The Emperor believes that the war situation is still unfavorable to the Italian army. The Italian army will encounter unexpected difficulties in the high mountains. New weapons cannot be used there. Furthermore, it is doubtful whether the native soldiers recruited by Italy in Eritrea and Italian Somaliland will be loyal and reliable if they engage in combat with their own kind. The Emperor finally spoke of Abyssinia's development, saying that it should proceed gradually and not seek speed. (Reuters, 26th)

The Abyssinian people in Addis Ababa are now awaiting the meeting of the Council of Administration of the League of Nations with a very calm attitude and have not expressed any xenophobic sentiments. Regarding the issue of arms imports, according to well-informed sources, Britain will not object to arms passing through its territory to Abyssinia. However, according to official sources, the import of arms into Abyssinia has been suspended for ten months. (Havas, 26th)

(Paris) Mr. Grillis, a correspondent for the Paris Echo in Rome, claims that Abyssinia has a well-organized army of 100,000 to 120,000 men, equipped with European equipment and trained by Belgian instructors. However, in terms of artillery, there are only a few batteries of old-fashioned artillery, about 500 machine guns. As for ammunition, a large quantity must have been stored in advance in some locations in the country's mountains for a long time. In addition, the new equipment available in the army is only a few tanks and some aircraft. Abyssinia has a population of about 10 million, of which 500,000 to 600,000 people, including women and children, at most about 1 million people, can serve the Emperor. The reporter also said: "Abyssinia's area is twice that of France. Its climate is hot and unbearable, and its terrain is mountainous. It is easy to put up a heroic and strong resistance against the invasion of a powerful neighbor. As for Italy, its army that has already opened up in East Africa currently has 120,000 men. Once the mobilized troops from the home country arrive, it will increase to 150,000 men. When the main battle starts in the future, its troop strength may be greatly increased or decreased. This army has a large number of modern equipment, especially tanks, machine gun vehicles, and aircraft. Forty airfields have been set up for reconnaissance and bombing aircraft to land. However, the use of this new air force may not immediately achieve final victory. Although Addis Ababa is only 750 kilometers away from the Italian army's airfield, Italian three-engine bombers carrying one ton of bombs can travel 2,000 kilometers and bomb it. However, the capital of Abyssinia is a city of 100,000 people, and even if it is destroyed, it will not do much harm. This matter is the same as when Napoleon I marched into Russia in 1812 and burned Moscow, which has nothing to do with the final victory of the war." (Havas, 27th)

New Franco-Italian Plan for Danube River Convention Said to be Proposed to Austria-Hungary and the Little Entente 48

(Rome) France and Italy have proposed a plan to Austria-Hungary and the Little Entente countries. It is said that the countries have expressed sympathy, so the Danube River Convention has been given a new life. The main points of the Franco-Italian plan are as follows: (1) Confirm the independence of Austria; (2) Declare that they will not interfere with each other, including propaganda, will not commit aggression, and will not assist aggressors; (3) If any signatory country violates the convention, the contracting countries will consult with each other. The draft has now been sent to Germany. It is said that Germany will not accept it unless the convention states that bilateral agreements are rejected. However, it is believed that even if the convention rejects this type of agreement, Germany will still hold other objections and not participate in this agreement. According to sources here, even if Germany does not join, the countries are still willing to proceed with the signing procedures. The Franco-Italian plan will also be notified to Britain and Poland. German Death Rate Increases 58

(Paris) According to the latest statistics released for the first four months of this year, the number of marriages in France has increased, and the number of divorces has decreased. However, a serious fact still exists, that is, the birth rate has decreased, and the death rate has increased. In the first four months, there were a total of 59,120 marriages, compared to 56,325 in the same period last year. There were 4,296 divorces, compared to 4,209 last year. There were only 166,509 births, compared to 176,962 last year. There were 200,046 deaths, compared to 189,244 last year. This number indicates that deaths exceeded births by 33,456 people, while the difference in the same period last year was only 12,281 people. (National Telegram, 26th)

Regulations for the Implementation of the Publication Law Under Review by the Executive Yuan Yesterday 62

(Nanjing) The new publication law, after being passed by the Legislative Yuan, has been submitted to the National Government for promulgation and implementation. The old law will be declared abolished on the date of promulgation and implementation of the new law. The regulations for the implementation of the new publication law, in accordance with Article 48 of the law, have been drafted by the Ministry of the Interior and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review. The Executive Yuan held a special meeting at 10:00 AM on the 27th to review the regulations. Executive Yuan Councillors Chen Nianzhong, Duanmu Kai, and Teng Gu, Ministry of the Interior Li Songfeng, Ministry of Education Jiang Fucong, and Ministry of Foreign Affairs Li Dijun were present. Chen Nianzhong presided over the meeting. After careful discussion, some minor revisions were made. The regulations will be submitted to the Executive Yuan meeting next Tuesday for approval and then promulgated, to be implemented simultaneously with the new law. It is reported that the full text of the regulations consists of 29 articles. During the review on the 27th, Article 15 of the draft was deleted and a new article was added, which contains interpretations of important terms in the new law, and the National Central Library was added as one of the agencies to which publications should be submitted for review. (Central News Agency dispatch, 27th)

(Nanjing) After the amended publication law was passed by the Legislative Yuan, the eight articles of the regulations for the implementation of the publication law were drafted by the relevant agencies and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. The Executive Yuan convened a review meeting on the morning of the 27th. The representatives attending were Chen Nianzhong, Duanmu Kai, and Teng Gu from the Executive Yuan, Li Dijun from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Jiang Fucong from the Ministry of Education, and Li Songfeng from the Ministry of the Interior. Chen Nianzhong presided over the meeting. As a result of the review, the regulations were completely approved. The regulations were formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 48 of the Publication Law, consisting of 29 articles. In addition to deleting Article 15 and paragraph 2 of Article 6, a new Article 11 was added. The main points of the content are: (1) If the content of a book or other publication that has been reviewed and approved does not match the approved manuscript, the Ministry of the Interior may confiscate it; (2) If, after a publication has been reviewed and approved, it is subject to the prohibition or restriction order stipulated in Article 12 of the Publication Law, it may still be confiscated; (3) The "prohibition disposition" mentioned in Article 28 of the Publication Law shall not be executed without the approval of the Ministry of the Interior. The Ministry of the Interior may, depending on the circumstances, impose a permanent or temporary prohibition. (Special dispatch, 27th)

(Nanjing) Minister of Justice Wang Yongbin, accompanied by Councillors Yang Peng, Secretary Qi Chen Daqi, Section Chiefs Wang Dengdi, Liao Weixun, and a total of seven staff members, departed from Nanjing at 7:00 PM on the 27th by Jinpu train northward. (Special dispatch, 27th)

(Nanjing) Wang Yongbin, accompanied by Yang Peng, Secretary Chen Daqiu, Section Chiefs Dengdi and Liao Wang Weixun of the Ministry of Justice, departed from Nanjing at 7:00 PM on the 27th by Jinpu train to inspect the judiciary. According to Wang, the purpose of this trip is to inspect the facilities and general situation after the reorganization of the trial levels in various places, and to urge the courts to clear up backlog cases and redress grievances of the people. He will first go to Shandong to inspect the Jinning, Tai'an, Jinan, and Qingdao courts, then proceed to Hebei to inspect the courts and prisons in Beijing and Tianjin, and then go to Suiyuan, Chahar, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Henan and other provinces to inspect places with convenient transportation. If time permits on the return journey, he will inspect the courts in Tongshan, Fengyang, and Bengbu in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces. The trip is expected to take about 40 days, returning to Nanjing no later than the beginning of September to attend the judicial conference. After the conference, he plans to inspect the provinces along the Yangtze River again, and in winter, he will make a trip to Guangdong and Guangxi and the southwestern provinces. He aims to inspect the actual judicial situation in all provinces of the country within these six months, so as to avoid sitting in the capital and issuing orders, which would be superficial and unrealistic for promoting the reform of the judiciary. (Central News Agency dispatch, 27th)

Terrible Flood Situation in Hanchuan: 98% of the County Submerged, 5,000 People Drowned, 60,000 Houses Collapsed - Report After Inspection by Ai Yuying of the Provincial Party Committee

Hankou Communication: This year's flood in Hubei Province is most severe in the Xiang River basin, and among the Xiang River basin, Fancheng, Zhongxiang, Tianmen, and Hanchuan are the most tragic. Although this reporter is stationed in Hankou and has been reporting news from various places to this newspaper from time to time, I regret that I have not been able to provide detailed information because I have not personally experienced it. In order to understand the disaster situation in various places, the Hubei Provincial Party Department specially dispatched member Ai Yuying to inspect the Xiang River basin. Yesterday, she arrived in Hanchuan and reported the inspection situation to the Provincial Party Department today. The report is very detailed. The report briefly states that starting from Wuchang, passing through Hanyang to Hanchuan, there is no land for more than 180 li. Arriving at Hanchuan County, mooring the boat on the embankment, refugees set up shacks and lived in a mixed way, and it was impossible to find a way to enter the city. According to the refugees on the embankment, there were still several feet of water in the city, so they returned to the boat to wait for Huang Zhiyuan, a cadre of the County Party Department, to come to the boat and ask him to guide them. First, they ascended Xiannv Mountain. The mountain has the tomb of Chu Lingyin Ziwen. According to the county chronicles, the top of the mountain is a square platform, which is where King Xiang of Chu entered the dream in Gaotang. Below is Lake Yaohan, covering an area of ​​more than 100 li, which bandits once used as a den. From the mountain overlooking the entire county, both the north and south banks are a vast expanse of water. Only one dike is still partially preserved, and Yanglinggou in the third district is not flooded. Then they went to the county seat to investigate and rescued about 4,000 disaster victims, all of whom were taken in by the county government. What they urgently need is not money but food and medicine. County Magistrate Zhou Yuwen supervised the construction of the dike and worked day and night for half a month, which was quite appreciated by the people. However, the Dike Construction Bureau, which was specifically responsible, was indifferent and did not make any preparations in advance, and cut corners on materials during the emergency rescue, which made the people extremely dissatisfied. As for the disaster, according to the investigation, it can be divided into three stages. On the morning of July 7, Yangchikou on the north bank of the Xiang River and Yanjiawan on the south bank collapsed at the same time. Both breaches were near the county seat. Jiangxiyuan, Mabou, Yaoeryuan, and Yahu on the north bank and Boziyuan on the south bank were all submerged. This was the first stage. On the morning of the 9th, the Xiang River flooded into the western part of the county due to the collapse of the Shangsangguan Dike in Zhongxiang Siyuan. The water was so large that the dikes could not be blocked. As a result, more than 200 dikes, accounting for two-thirds of the entire county's area north of the Xiang River, were almost completely flooded within two days. The county seat was also affected on the 10th, destroying three sections of the city wall. This was the second stage. At noon on the 13th, the Yangtze River water poured into the southern part of the county through Duntou, and at the same time, the Cekou River, a southern tributary of the Han River, overflowed to the east and joined the Yangtze River water. The most important Nanping Dike sank to the bottom of the water, and the nearby small dikes were completely destroyed. This was the third stage. 1.4 million mu of the county's 1.5 million mu of land were flooded, accounting for 98% of the county's area. Of the 390,000 people in the county, 320,000 were disaster victims. The number of people who died in the water could not be accurately determined, but the Cao Lake coast in the northern part of the county was the most severely affected. In the Penggang Lake township in the east of the county, 300 to 400 people drowned. Doubu Township, Xiazi Township, and Heitan Township were even lower and were the first to be hit by the water from Zhongxiang and Tianmen. The number of deaths was about 3,000 to 4,000. The disaster victims who did not die gathered on the dikes, exposed to the sun and water vapor, eating and sleeping in the open air. Epidemics spread, and the number of people who died from cholera and heatstroke was countless. It can be assumed that the total number of deaths was 5,000. In addition, of the 80,000 houses in the county, more than 60,000 were washed away or collapsed. Rice was produced in the northern dikes and cotton was produced along the Xiang River, all of which were lost to the flood. The spring harvest of soybeans and wheat, as well as silver, clothes, livestock, and farming tools, were all lost due to the lack of time to rescue them. It was truly an unprecedented catastrophe. (24th)

Detailed Information on the Yanshi Flood Presented by the County Magistrate to the Henan-Shandong Supervisory Office 92

Luoyang Communication: In the first ten days of this month, the river water rose sharply, the Yanshi city dike breached, and the entire city was submerged, causing serious disasters. The following is a selection of the information presented by Yang Zhaofang, the magistrate of Yanshi County, to the Henan-Shandong District Supervisory Office on the 17th of this month. Reading it will show the detailed situation of the county's flood: (1) Topography of the county: The county is mountainous in the north and south, with the Yi and Luo Rivers running through the center. Districts 1 and 2 belong to the Mangshan Mountains, districts 5, 6, and 7 rely on the Songshan Mountains, the northern part of districts 3 and 5, the southern part of districts 1 and 2, and all of district 4 are located between the Yi and Luo Rivers, called the "Jiahe Beach," which are all in the Yi and Luo River basins. The county seat is located on the north bank of the Yi River, about 5 li from the confluence of the Yi and Luo Rivers, and the terrain is low. (2) Largest mountains and rivers: The largest mountain range in the county is the Songshan Mountains, and the largest river is the Yi and Luo Rivers. They merge south of the city and are still called the Luo River. (3) Reasons for the flood: The Yi River originates in the Wawa Mountains in Henan, flows through Songxian and Yiyang, and enters Yanshi. The Luo River originates in the foothills of the Shaohua Mountains in Shaanxi, flows through Luonan, Lushi, Luoning, and enters Yanshi in the east, merging with the Luo River five li south of the county seat. Due to continuous rain in the upper reaches, mountain floods occurred frequently. The downstream reaches to Gongyi have the Black Stone Pass, with rocks on both sides of the river, and the Longhai Railway bridge crosses north and south. Whenever the river water rises sharply, floating debris blocks the flow excessively. In addition, the Yellow River is silting up and rising at the same time, making it difficult to discharge the water, resulting in accumulated water. In the past, when the Luo and Yi Rivers rose sharply, the counties along the river suffered disasters, with Yanshi being the most severe and the upstream counties being lighter. (4) Period of flooding: It rained heavily on the afternoon of July 7, and the river water rose sharply on the first day of the 8th month. The city dike breached before the hour of Wei, and the entire city was submerged before the hour of Shen. (5) Prior prevention: The county seat is located in a low-lying area. Whenever there are mountain floods and river water rises sharply in the upper reaches, the county seat suffers the most. In the 13th year of Qianlong in the Qing Dynasty, the city collapsed due to water, and dikes were built to protect it after the water subsided. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, the dikes breached, and only the southeastern half of the city was two feet deep in water. In view of the floods in previous years, the dikes were repaired once a year, and half of the soil was piled on the southwest dike to prevent emergencies. This time, on the night of the 7th, the river water rose sharply. The county government immediately summoned the heads of the Zhongshan Town and the heads of various districts, as well as strong men, to carry sandbags, wood, branches, stones, and reeds overnight to protect the dikes, and added earth to build dikes. On the morning of the 8th, the wind and rain intensified, and the water became more urgent. The strong men from Tanghua and Tangquan townships in the north of the city, as well as the police and political police, and the staff of various agencies and merchants, all rose up to rescue the dikes. However, the water flow was turbulent, the rain did not stop, and the northeast dike breached in several places before the hour of Wei. There was no way to rescue the dikes, and a reward of 1,000 yuan was offered, but no one dared to respond. Later, the south dike overflowed, and the west dike also successively issued warnings, collapsing six or seven zhang. At that time, the water inside the dike was more than a foot high, and the situation was dangerous. There was no way to block it. County Magistrate Yang Zhaofang led the people to retreat to the city defense, placing sandbags and soil bags everywhere. Before the end of the hour of Wei, the outer city and city walls outside the east gate were washed down, followed by the south tower, and then the north gate. By the time the west gate was flooded, it was already the hour of Shen. At that time, the water in the four gates was like ten thousand horses galloping, and the entire city was submerged in an instant. (6) Evacuation in case of failure to prevent the flood: When the east gate was flooded, the people were ordered to evacuate through the north gate, but less than three-tenths of them were able to do so. The rest either fled to the north city tower and Wenchang Pavilion, or climbed trees, or squatted on the collapsed rooftops, drifting with the water. The county government personnel retreated to the back building of the county government, and the teachers and students of the education bureau and middle school retreated to the pavilions of the bureau and school. On the morning of the 9th, they made wooden rafts and crossed out of the north gate. (7) Damage to files of the county government and various agencies: The files of the county government were moved to the back building when the city dike breached and overflowed on the 8th. However, there was only one building, and the important ones were stored first. However, before they were finished, the water rushed in and the file room was flooded. The ones stored upstairs were trampled on because there were too many people in distress, causing considerable losses. The files of various agencies were also incomplete. (8) Number of deaths in the whole city and districts: The number of deaths in the city was more than 230, and more than 300 livestock. The remaining bodies that were crushed are being salvaged. The number of deaths in various districts is currently under investigation. (9) Houses submerged in the whole county: 95% of the houses in the city have been submerged, totaling more than 10,000. The various districts are also under investigation. (10) Cultivated land submerged in the whole county: Approximately 2,000 qing. (11) Amount of property loss in the whole county: Approximately more than 4 million. (12) Relocation of the county government and various agencies: The county government is temporarily located in Beiyaocun, about one li north of the city. The future relocation has not yet been determined and a suitable location is being properly discussed. (13) Collapse of city walls: Approximately 800 zhang. (14) After the disaster, the Provincial Relief Association allocated 1,000 yuan and distributed it to the Disaster Relief Committee on a per capita basis, with 20 cents for adults and 10 cents for children. If it was not enough, the number of strong men was reduced. According to Guo Fangwu, a member of the Yuxi Disaster Relief Branch, District Commissioner Sheng of the 10th district convened a water conservancy meeting in the district to raise 4,000 yuan to repair the dikes inside the Luo River and telegraphed 1,000 yuan for emergency relief to Yanshi. The funds have been advanced by the Luoyang Finance Committee and are expected to arrive in Yanshi in two or three days. (15) Most severely affected areas: In addition to Chengguan, the 3rd and 4th districts are the most severely affected, followed by the 1st and 2nd districts, and then the 5th district. Number of affected households in each district: A total of 1,364 households in 14 districts in Chengguan have been affected by the flood. 1,207 households have been accounted for, and 157 households are missing. The other districts are still under investigation. (16) Number of people in each district awaiting relief: The number of disaster victims in Chengguan that have been investigated is more than 12,000, and the other districts are still under investigation. (17) Number of people displaced due to the disaster in each district: Approximately 1% of those affected have moved to Kaifeng, Luoyang, and Zhengzhou, and the rest are still living in safe areas north and south of the county. (18) Area submerged in the whole county: One-half of the area in the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd districts was submerged, all of the 4th district was submerged, and one-third of the 5th district was submerged. Current water situation in the city: The water in Dongguan is more than one zhang deep, the water in Nanguan is about two zhang deep, the water in Beiguan is two or three chi deep, and the water in Xiguan is more than five chi deep. Deaths of personnel of the county government and various agencies: One orderly of the county government, one water pattern observer stationed in Yanshi from the Third Water Conservancy Bureau, four soldiers of the security team, and one sanitation worker of the Public Security Bureau. (19) Damage along the way during the flood: Telephone and telegraph lines, the Yanshi-Dengfeng, Yanshi-Gongyi, and Yanshi-Luoyang county roads were mostly damaged. Current traffic situation: Telephone and telegraph communications have been cut off, and the post office moved to Yaotou Village on the 12th of this month to begin operations. (20) Escape of prisoners in the prison and detention center: A total of 45 prisoners escaped and are being pursued. (21) Regarding epidemic prevention: In addition to the three types of drugs sent by the Provincial Relief Association, which have been distributed separately, the county hospital has been ordered to purchase epidemic prevention drugs and administer epidemic prevention injections. (July 22)

Gansu Province Continues to Abolish Excessive Levies 93

Abolishing 58 Types of Taxes and Levies Annually Reduces Revenue by Over 110,000 Yuan

Lanzhou Dispatch: Since Mr. Zhu Jingzhou, the Director of the Gansu Provincial Department of Finance, implemented the first phase of abolishing excessive taxes and levies in January of this year, he has been actively engaged in investigations to prepare for the second phase. According to the current investigation results, those taxes and levies that are considered excessive and urgently need to be abolished include 55 types of special consumption taxes, which generate a total annual revenue of 52,831.28 yuan. Additionally, a 10% voluntary donation attached to the tobacco and alcohol tax generates 47,600 yuan. Furthermore, Sichuan leaf cigarettes and tobacco concentrate generate an annual revenue of 10,111 yuan. (The original cigarette inspection fee in Gansu Province was completely abolished at the end of June and replaced with a unified tax. This item refers to Sichuan-produced leaf cigarettes and their raw materials, which are not included in the unified tax reform. Because they are domestic products and belong to handicrafts, a request has been submitted to the provincial government for exemption.) The above three items comprise a total of 58 tax items, with an annual revenue of 110,541.28 yuan. This has been approved by the provincial government and will be fully implemented starting from July 1st of this year. The provincial government has also submitted the matter to the Executive Yuan, the Chairman's Headquarters, and the Ministry of Finance for record-keeping. However, Gansu is inherently a poor province. The first phase abolished excessive levies amounting to over 380,000 yuan, and now another 110,000 yuan has been reduced, making the budget even more insufficient. Mr. Zhu believes that the abolition of excessive levies is of utmost importance to the national economy and people's livelihood, and he has no choice but to implement it despite the difficulties. He hopes that the central government will provide substantial subsidies to alleviate the financial difficulties and to address the detailed process of abolishing excessive levies. At the same time, he has issued orders to all tax bureaus to comply and has also sent letters to chambers of commerce to forward to local chambers of commerce and to inform the citizens. The list of names and tax amounts for the second phase of abolishing excessive levies is as follows:

Jiading: Impoverished and Ill, Taking His Own Life by Drowning

On June 21st, the Jiaxiang Steamboat was sailing near Shitumeng when, at dusk, a passenger suddenly jumped into the river. Rescue efforts were unsuccessful. The next morning, the body surfaced, but no one claimed it. After investigation by the county government, it was confirmed that the deceased had drowned himself. A coffin was provided by the local government for burial in the public cemetery. On the 26th, the deceased's son inquired at the steamboat company about the situation and identified a straw hat left behind as belonging to his father. He stated that his father had taken his own life by drowning due to poverty and illness, which prevented him from working.

Wuxi: Public Security Bureau Cracks Down on a Major Den

In Beimaopeng, Huishan, in this county, there is a Juesheng Temple, also known as Qilü Chan Forest or Maomiao Temple. The temple is located in a secluded area, comprising about thirty rooms. It has seven or eight monks and flourishing incense offerings. The abbot, named Yingru, is over forty years old and specializes in committing adultery and other crimes. He colludes with the lay monk Changhe in the temple, engaging in all sorts of evil deeds. They have a secret room and underground chamber in the temple, equipped with opium pipes, where they gather to gamble. Women with attractive appearances who come to burn incense and pray are seduced into the room and raped, sometimes even by violent means. Recently, a guest monk named Zhirun secretly reported the situation to the Public Security Bureau, stating that the monk Yingru also went to the Huishan area at night to exhume graves and steal coffins. The bureau dispatched inspector Ge Xinde, clerk Chen Zhongshou, and a large number of police officers, accompanied by Zhilun, on a roundabout route up the mountain on a dark night. Zhirun called open the back door of the temple, and the police rushed in. In the abbot's room, they pushed open a wooden wall and entered a secret room, where the monks Changhe, Zhiyin, and Shuchun from neighboring temples were gambling. They were immediately captured and a set of dominoes was confiscated. Then they went to the station room, where a servant climbed through a food delivery hole and confiscated opium pipes and other items. Later, they discovered a richly decorated secret room, entered it, and apprehended the monk Yingru. They also found qipaos, women's silk shoes, face powder, opium paste, and opium paraphernalia. Finally, they discovered an underground chamber under a movable floor in the room, where a middle-aged woman was found naked and asleep on a couch. She was also arrested and identified herself as Jiang Wenzhen (also known as Miss Jin). She readily admitted to having an affair with the monk. After the police finished searching, they took Yingru, Changhe, Zhiyin, and Jiang Wenzhen, along with the evidence, to the bureau. The monk Shuchun was left to guard the temple gate and was not taken to the bureau. Later, section member Zhang from the third section of the Public Security Bureau conducted a preliminary hearing. The defendants' testimonies were cunning, and it was decided to submit the case to the county government for further investigation and handling.

Yangzhou: Riverbank Collapses Again for Over 110 Zhang

Recently, the riverbank in Liuwei has been collapsing frequently due to the rising tide. At 3:00 AM on the 25th, the east end of Liuwei collapsed again for over 110 zhang, causing the ferry boat of the Zhenyang Pujun Ferry, which was docked there, to drift away with the waves. Staff from the ferry office worked overnight to find it with a charitable ferry boat and finally found it near the Doutian Temple at dawn. Therefore, to avoid danger to passengers, the Pujun Ferry Bureau has temporarily suspended ticket sales for Liuwei.

Nantong: Expansion of the Fourth Prison Implemented

The Jiangsu Fourth Prison in Tongcheng, which houses male and female offenders sentenced to more than three years from Tongruhai counties, is expanding its prison cells to accommodate a large number of prisoners who will be transferred from the Suzhou Third Sub-prison. The expansion has been approved by the High Court.

Hangzhou: Zhegan Railway Extends to Shangrao

The track-laying project for the Nanyu section of the Zhegan Railway was only four kilometers away from Shangrao yesterday. It is expected to be completed today (the 28th). A trial run is planned for tonight, and ticket sales will officially begin on August 1st. Passenger trains between Hangzhou and Yushan will directly reach Shangrao, with daily round trips in both directions, providing convenience for travelers.

Safety Measures for Qianjiang Pier

The plum blossom piles at the Yidu Pier on the north and south banks of the Qiantang River have been hollowed out by saltwater and shipworms and are collapsing. Those that have not yet collapsed are also quite dangerous. The Department of Construction, recognizing the Qiantang River as a vital transportation hub between eastern and western Zhejiang, convened a meeting of relevant agencies to discuss rescue measures. Recognizing that any accident at the Qiantang River pier would have a significant impact on traveler safety, it was decided to notify vehicles to temporarily cease operations to prevent danger. The Water Conservancy Bureau will formulate two types of safety measures: temporary and permanent. Six iron anchors, each weighing approximately two tons, will be purchased from Shanghai and placed at the two north and south piers to temporarily maintain safety. After the autumn tide, two pairs of reinforced concrete pillars will be built to ensure permanent safety.

Local News

Ministry of Finance Promulgates Measures for Exchanging Old Stamp Tax Stamps; Starting This Month, Staggered Exchange of New Stamps Is Allowed for Self-Use Only in This Store 94

The old stamp tax stamps in this city have been registered by the Chamber of Commerce in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Finance for some time. The exchange measures have been officially announced after repeated telegrams from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce urging the matter. The following is a record:

Ministry Telegram: Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce for review. Applications for old stamp tax stamps that have been registered by various provinces have been submitted to the Ministry one after another and are about to be fully reviewed. It is appropriate to schedule an exchange to demonstrate credibility. Six articles of measures for exchanging old stamp tax stamps are hereby formulated and promulgated for implementation. In addition to sending telegrams separately, the original measures are hereby issued with the telegram for your compliance. Regarding how to handle old stamps affixed by merchants and the public, please wait for further instructions by telegram. Ministry of Finance Seal

Measures: (1) Old stamp tax stamps that have been approved for registration in various provinces and cities (cities are limited to those directly under the Executive Yuan) shall be exchanged for new stamp tax stamps starting in July, according to the following standards: those within 10,000 yuan shall be exchanged within one month; those within 20,000 yuan shall be exchanged in two months on average; those within 40,000 yuan shall be exchanged in three months on average; those within 60,000 yuan shall be exchanged in four months on average; those within 100,000 yuan shall be exchanged in five months on average; and those exceeding 100,000 yuan shall be exchanged in six months on average. (2) Old stamp tax stamps that have been registered and approved in various provinces and cities, except for those with a value of less than 10,000 yuan, which should be exchanged at once, should be collected first by the chambers of commerce in each province and city, and after detailed verification by the provincial stamp tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus, they should be sealed and stored in the respective chambers of commerce for the purpose of exchanging new stamp tax stamps on a monthly basis in accordance with the provisions of Article 1. (3) The new stamp tax stamps to be exchanged by each province and city each month shall be verified and issued by the Ministry of Finance in accordance with the standards prescribed in Article 1 to the stamp tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus of each province for exchange. The old stamp tax stamps collected each month shall be listed and submitted to the Ministry for destruction. (4) When exchanging new stamp tax stamps each month, the chamber of commerce of each province and city shall, together with the provincial stamp tobacco and alcohol tax bureau, extract the number of old stamp tax stamps from the sealed old stamp tax stamps in accordance with the standard number specified in Article 1 and submit them to the provincial bureau for collection and destruction. (5) The number to be exchanged by each store each month shall be allocated by the chamber of commerce of each province and city according to the amount of stamps in stock. (6) The new stamp tax stamps to be exchanged by each province and city shall be uniformly stamped by the Ministry of Finance with the name of each province to indicate the difference. These new stamps are only allowed for self-use by the stores. If there is any private sale or other fraudulent activity, and it is verified to be true, the stamp tax stamps shall be confiscated.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Announcement: Loan Application Forms Begin to Be Issued; Industry and Commerce Revival Committee Handles; Ministry of Finance Explains Mortgage Loans 95

The Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee sent a letter to the Cloth Chamber of Commerce for distribution, stating that it would produce application forms for small industrial and commercial credit loans. The Chamber of Commerce has decided to handle it through the Industry and Commerce Revival Committee and will begin issuing them starting on the 29th. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has notified all members and announced the matter to all factories and firms in the city. The details are as follows:

Letter from the Loan Committee: The Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Regarding the 5 million yuan small credit loan to assist industry and commerce in Shanghai, the Ministry of Finance previously ordered this committee to review and release the loans. Active preparations have been made and the fourth meeting of this committee resolved to send the credit loan application forms, etc., to the municipal chamber of commerce for distribution to the various trade associations, for applicants in each industry to fill out and submit to this committee for investigation and review. Factories and firms that are not members of trade associations may also obtain application forms from the municipal chamber of commerce, fill them out, and submit them to this committee for review. The above loan has been resolved at the sixth meeting of this committee on the 22nd of this month and is scheduled to begin lending on August 1st. We are sending three thousand copies of the application forms and accompanying form instructions printed by this committee in advance for your review, collection, and distribution. If it is insufficient, please notify this committee at any time for further delivery. If necessary regarding the procedures for filling out the application form, this committee will assign specialists to reside in your committee to guide and explain to the applicants. We hope you will take note of this."

Starting Tomorrow: After receiving the documents from the Industry and Commerce Loan Committee on the 27th, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce immediately notified all members and issued a public notice. However, because the procedures for filling out the application form still require the committee to send personnel to instruct, and all procedures must be prepared, it was decided to start collecting from the Industry and Commerce Revival Committee starting on the 29th of this month, i.e., next Monday, and Wang Yansong, the director of the Revival Committee, will publicly instruct in the Chamber of Commerce assembly hall at 9:00 AM on the 29th.

Chamber of Commerce Announcement: The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce hereby announces the matter of collecting blank application forms for small credit loans. The Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee is undertaking the matter of small credit loans to assist industry and commerce in Shanghai. The committee has prepared all the application forms and forms that applicants should fill out and has transferred them to this committee. All industrial and commercial enterprises in this city who wish to apply for a small credit loan can go directly to the Revival Industry and Commerce Committee attached to the second floor of this committee to collect the blank forms and report in the prescribed format. The time for going to the committee to collect the forms is from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day except holidays. This announcement.

Ministry of Finance Interpretation: The Chamber of Commerce previously requested the Ministry of Finance to explain whether the procedure for loans to assist industry and commerce, which are released by various banks and firms, needs special procedures or is no different from mortgage loans. The Ministry of Finance replied with document Qian Zi No. 6421, stating that the review and approval of small industrial and commercial credit loans should be reported to the Loan Committee, and the lending industry should refer to Article 1 of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Detailed Rules approved by the committee and submitted to the Ministry for approval. Although mortgage loans are lent by various banks and firms, Article 2 of the Loan Detailed Rules stipulates that after this loan is reviewed and approved by the committee, the committee will issue treasury bonds as a second guarantee for the loan amount, and Article 7 of the Ministry's Lending Principles stipulates that the monthly interest rate for bank loans to assist industry and commerce shall not exceed eight percent. If the situation of the factory or firm cannot bear the full monthly interest rate, it may request the Ministry to approve a subsidy of two percent monthly interest, etc. Therefore, since the committee issues treasury bonds as a second guarantee for this mortgage loan and can request approval to subsidize the monthly interest rate, it is obviously different from ordinary mortgage loans. Applicants can request to follow the rules promulgated by the Ministry for monthly interest, and it cannot be said that there is no basis. Please note.

Yu Qiaqing Resigns from Two Positions: Resigns as Chairman of the Association and Standing Director of the Cooperative 98

Mr. Yu Qiaqing, a leader in the shipping industry, has sent letters resigning from his positions as Chairman of the Shanghai Steamboat Industry Association and Standing Director of the China Shipping Cooperative. The original text of the resignation letters is as follows:

Letter Resigning from Chairman of the Association: Since the Shanghai Shipping Association was reorganized into the Shipping Industry Association and renamed the Steamboat Industry Association, I have been honored to be elected by my colleagues to preside over the association's affairs for eight years. This year, the China Shipping Cooperative was established, and I was again elected as a non-governmental director. I did not dare to decline because the matter was voluntary and concerned my personal interests. Our country's shipping industry is known to be immature. Over the years, although the number of ships has gradually increased on the surface, the actual business has been declining. Recently, due to the decline of rural areas and the urgency of finance, the shipping industry has reached a dead end. As a leader in the non-governmental shipping industry, I feel obliged to help others, seek relief on the one hand, and seek survival on the other. This is not the time for me to decline in this critical moment of survival. However, since the China Merchants Group was nationalized and withdrew from the association, there has been an additional layer of relations. Although the government authorities have made every effort to appeal, they have not received practical benefits. Shipping colleagues have also failed to understand the difficulties. The establishment of the Shipping Administration Bureau was originally advocated by shipping merchants, and the revival of the Merchant Marine School was also agreed upon by shipping merchants, who observed the increase of a three percent ton banknote surcharge. Even these two things have been criticized as self-inflicted. The shipping cooperative is the only way to save ourselves at present and is fully endorsed by me and my colleagues. However, after designing and preparing for nearly a year, it has not yet been realized. After careful analysis, it is because the situation is not both ways and there are different views. If you are not careful, you will be used by others. In this situation, I have neither won the sympathy of the government nor met the expectations of my colleagues. I feel very panic. If this continues, there is no way to proceed. After repeated thinking, I have no choice but to give way to the virtuous and express my sincerity. I hope you will understand. Sincerely, Yu Hede, July 24, 24th year.

Letter Resigning from the Cooperative: Since the establishment of our cooperative, three months have passed. I was honored to be elected as a standing director. However, for the past three months, there have been no concrete measures. If this continues, I feel ashamed of my colleagues. I have already resigned from my position as a standing committee member and chairman of the Steamboat Industry Association. I should also resign from my position as a standing director and director of this cooperative. I hereby send this letter to request your approval and elect a capable person. To the China Shipping Cooperative, Yu Hede, July 14, 24th year.

Ministry of Railways Stipulates Procedures for On-Board Ticket Supplements; Railway Bureau Has Already Instructed the Traffic Department to Comply 100

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating that according to a case presented by the Ministry's Business Department, the 22nd proposal of the 9th National Railway Transportation Conference, proposed by the Ping-Sui Railway, concerned "regulations on the handling of original tickets after passengers traveling beyond their designated station or class have supplemented their tickets," and the 24th proposal, proposed by the Hunan-Hubei Railway, concerned "whether or not passenger tickets should be returned to passengers after they have supplemented their tickets on board," and the 23rd proposal, proposed by the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, concerned "requesting regulations on ticket supplementation methods." These thirteen cases were discussed together, and the conference resolved in the 105th resolution that (1) For passengers traveling beyond their designated station, in addition to supplementing their tickets or supplementing their tickets and being fined in accordance with Article 47 of the Passenger Transport Regulations, the original tickets should be uniformly collected, and the following statement should be noted in the first copy of the supplement: "Ticket No. [number] of [class] from [station] to [station] has been collected." The collected tickets should be attached to the second copy of the supplement and sent along with the payment receipt to the station master of the station where the ticket inspector is stationed for verification by the accounting department. (2) For passengers traveling beyond their designated class, in addition to supplementing their tickets and being fined in accordance with Article 47 of the Passenger Transport Regulations, the original tickets should be collected, and the following statement should be noted in the first copy of the supplement: "Ticket No. [number] of [class] from [station] to [station] has already been collected." The collected tickets should be attached to the first copy of the supplement and sent along with the payment receipt to the station master of the station where the ticket inspector is stationed for verification by the accounting department. The third copy of the supplement should leave a blank space for filling in and submitting to the Statistics Committee of the Unified Accounting System for format changes and implementation by all railways." It is still feasible and should be followed. In addition to separate orders, you should immediately comply with this order. It is understood that the Railway Bureau has already instructed the Traffic Department to comply.

Macgen Road Depot Extends Free Storage Period 102

The free storage period for goods at various stations of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways was originally set at seven days for incoming goods and three days for outgoing goods. However, the Macgen Road Depot, due to previous congestion, had reduced the storage period for incoming goods from seven days to five days, while the storage period for outgoing goods remained at three days. At the same time, the storage fees for all types of goods of the fourth class and below were uniformly charged at the third-class storage fee rate to restrict storage. Now, the Traffic Department, due to the poor soybean harvest this year, has found that incoming goods at the depot are not very active, and all warehouses have vacancies. With the approval of the bureau, starting from August, the free storage period for incoming goods at the Macgen Road Depot will be temporarily extended to seven days, and the storage fees for the fourth class and below will continue to be charged at the original rates to attract more business.

Labor Dispute at Huachang Coir Fiber Factory: Misunderstanding Leads to Assault on Workers 103

Dagong News Agency reports that since the Huachang Coir Fiber Factory in Pudong, Shanghai, suspended its film department operations, it has sparked a backlash from the factory's workers. The Shanghai Coir Fiber Workers' Union petitioned the party and government authorities for relief. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau approved the resumption of work as usual, but the factory refused to accept it, and the two sides were deadlocked. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning (the 27th) at around 9:00 AM, a large team of over 40 police officers, led by Inspector He of the Tangqiao Police Station, forcibly shipped out goods. Simultaneously, the factory sent staff member Xu Zukang to the Coir Fiber Workers' Union to request that people be sent to ship the goods. The union's executive director Ji Hao led more than ten warehouse workers to unload the goods at the factory, but they were assaulted by the police, including union director Ji Hao and workers Wang Jinrong, Shao Tianzhong, Zhu Jinde, Xu Ashun, Weng Zenghua, Qu Zucheng, Sun Acheng, He Jusheng, Wang Jinfu, and Ma Fulin, among others. Ji Hao and Wang Jinrong suffered the most severe injuries. After receiving the report, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions, considering the seriousness of the situation, dispatched Wang Renwu of the Social Affairs Bureau's Mediation Division and Wan Banghe, a cadre of the Federation of Trade Unions, to Pudong to investigate. In addition to immediately sending the injured workers to Nanyang Hospital for treatment, they will schedule a formal mediation. The Federation of Trade Unions will also convene an emergency meeting to discuss assistance and mediation measures.

Reports on the Tragic Flood Conditions in Various Provinces 106

Xu Shiying telegraphed Shanghai, reporting on the inspection of the Jiangxi disaster: "Wang Yilao and I respectfully ask for your understanding. I respectfully accepted your repeated telegrams inviting me to inspect the disaster. I left Hunan late last night and arrived in Hubei at noon today. I have somewhat discussed the relief plan with Chairman Zhang and Director He. I immediately boarded the Jianghua ship and arrived in Xun [Jiujiang] the next day. The floodwaters in the urban area have gradually receded, and epidemic prevention is extremely important. The Yangtze River is relatively stable, but the dikes of the inland lakes north of the river are collapsing due to the backflow of water from the breach in the Mahua Dike. The northerly wind has been quite noticeable in recent days. The Hengmian Dike of the Chugong Dike in Jiujiang County is particularly precarious. Within the dike are tens of thousands of acres of farmland, with agricultural products worth at least two million yuan, and the harvest is imminent. If it collapses, it will have a significant impact on Xunshi [Jiujiang] trade. Director Yan of the Jiangxi Water Conservancy Bureau is working day and night to reinforce the dikes, with the support of Chairman Xiong. I transferred to Nanchang in the evening and arrived at Chou [1-3 AM], where I discussed everything with Chairman Xiong. This morning, I took a boat to inspect the disaster situation in Duyang and other counties. I departed from Xun [Jiujiang] today to rush back to the capital on the day of Jian [August 1st] to present a general overview and prepare a report for submission as soon as possible, in order to facilitate overall planning. Furthermore, the Central Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Management Committee will formally be established on the 30th. I respectfully submit this telegram. Your brother, Bi Ying, bows. Youmao [5-7 AM] sees five."

Hundreds of thousands of starving people are exposed to the wind and eat in the open, on the verge of death. Your association has a charitable heart. We sincerely request you to generously donate large sums of money for relief. We are endlessly grateful." Please reply to us promptly regarding your plans. We are extremely eager to await your orders." Furthermore, a telegram was received from the headquarters reporting that the relief team has arrived in Shandong and is proceeding to Juye, Yuncheng, Jiaxiang, and other counties. The entire city is flooded, and the water level in Jinjia and other areas has recently risen again. The Yellow River mouth between Zhen and Yuncheng is being investigated and urgently relieved. Due to the vastness of the disaster area, there are insufficient teams to allocate. More relief team members have been dispatched from Jinan to be divided into districts for relief. However, the roads are muddy, and cars cannot pass. They must first go to Jining and then hire small cars or boats to detour. The roads are obstructed, and it will take three days to reach the disaster area. It is reported that after receiving the telegram, the office has scheduled an emergency meeting for yesterday to discuss relief measures.

The Chinese Jisheng Society recently received telegrams from Xiangyang and Fancheng counties in Hubei, stating, "During the summer flood season this year, continuous rain has caused a disaster. Floods have erupted and spread endlessly. The Yangtze and Han rivers have risen simultaneously, and the dikes along the banks have all collapsed. In particular, Fancheng and Xiangyang in the upper reaches of the Han River have suffered complete inundation, with water levels rising ten feet. People have become fish, and the areas of Hanmian and Qianjiang have been turned into swamps. The rapid currents have swept away residents who were unable to escape, and an estimated tens of thousands have died. Corpses are floating everywhere, a sight too unbearable to witness. The situation is extremely tragic. Wuhan, located at the confluence of the two rivers, has already seen the effects of the disaster. The original dikes are all in imminent danger, and people are working day and night to prevent them from collapsing, hoping to escape danger. However, the disaster is extremely severe, surpassing even the disaster of 20 years ago. The disaster victims are unable to save themselves. We earnestly request all of you to have compassion and provide generous relief, either by allocating public funds or donating from your private pockets, to provide urgent relief. We appeal in unison, with utmost urgency," etc. The report of the submersion of Yanshi County in Henan has just arrived, and now Xiangyang and Fancheng counties in Hubei have suffered complete inundation. Although the disaster conditions in other provinces such as Hunan, Anhui, Shandong, and Jiangsu may differ, the consecutive years of disasters and droughts have left ten households with nine empty. Now, they have been flooded again, and some counties have suffered complete inundation. The heart aches when writing about it, and the situation is indescribable. We only hope that compassionate and virtuous people at home and abroad will rise up and provide immediate relief, so that they will not all fill the gullies.

The Hubei Provincial Association in Shanghai received a reply telegram from the Relief Affairs Committee yesterday, which stated, "To Chairman Guan Wang and Vice Chairmen Liu of the Hubei Provincial Association in Shanghai: We have received your telegram and learned of the severe flood disaster in your province. We are deeply saddened. According to previous reports, we have telegraphed the Hubei Provincial Government, the Hubei Provincial Relief Affairs Committee, and the Hubei Provincial Flood Relief Headquarters to promptly report the area and losses in all disaster areas in detail for verification. The request has been approved. In addition to further urging them to facilitate overall planning, we are replying by telegram for your information." The Relief Affairs Committee, and also received a reply letter from the World Red Swastika Society, which stated, "Dear Sirs: We received your letter yesterday, along with a telegram from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce. We respectfully learned that your province has suffered a severe flood disaster. We previously received urgent telegrams from Mr. He Hengfu and Mr. Huang Wenzhi of the Wuhan Joint Office of our society, and we immediately remitted 1,000 yuan to provide urgent relief and telegraphed the branches in Marukiang, Anqing, Wuhu, and Datong to salvage the floating corpses of those drowned in Tianmen and Gucheng counties. The Nanjing branch sent a team to Hubei for relief, and we telegraphed our headquarters and sent circulars to branches throughout the country, urging them to donate. We are replying with this special letter for your information." Signed by the United General Office of the Southeast Branches of the World Red Swastika Society.

Completion of the Jiangsu-Shanghai Highway: Private Cars Already Allowed; Long-Distance Buses to Begin Service on the 10th 107

The Xinxin News Agency reports that the Jiangsu-Shanghai Highway was completed last month, and private cars are already allowed. The Jiangsu provincial authorities have set August 10th as the official date for long-distance buses to begin service. Passengers traveling from Kunshan to the Lianglu Garden Hotel can travel to the bridge bank as described above, and then travel south for about a mile through the countryside, or call ahead and the hotel will send a yacht (gasoline boat for groups) to pick them up at the bridge bank. Raven Submits a Response to the U.S. Court 108

The "North China Daily News" reports that Mr. He Fu, the liquidator of the U.S. Feng Bank and other three companies, previously filed a petition with the U.S. Court in China on June 29th, seeking to recover from Mr. Raven, the manager of the former U.S. Feng Bank, Meidong Bank, Puyi Real Estate Company, and Puyi Bank, the bonuses granted by the U.S. Feng Bank, Meidong Bank, and Puyi Real Estate Company in January 1932, totaling 405,000 taels of silver. Yesterday afternoon (the 26th), Mr. Raven submitted a response to the U.S. Court. The main points are as follows: The defendant admits that he has owned and managed a large portion of the voting capital of Puyi Bank for the past five years and admits that Puyi Bank currently owns and manages a large portion of the voting capital of Meidong Bank. Meidong Bank, in turn, has owned and managed a large portion of the voting capital of the U.S. Feng Bank for the past five years and is doing so currently. However, the defendant denies ever managing the bank during any period in the past five years. On January 12, 1932, the bank's assets exceeded its liabilities by more than twice the amount, excluding capital surplus and undistributed dividends. At that time, the cash on hand and the cash deposited in various banks accounted for approximately 44% of the deposits received. At that time and for some time thereafter, the price of its stock in the Shanghai market rose to more than twice its original value. The defendant denies that he was managing the bank on January 12, 1932. As for the bank's directors, they were elected by the shareholders at any time and were able to independently decide everything, without being directly or indirectly controlled by the defendant in any way. When the board of directors passed the resolution on bonuses, the defendant attended the meeting at the beginning, but he did not know that the issue was being considered beforehand. The defendant did not apply for this bonus, and he only learned of the resolution after the meeting was over. The defendant later paid 135,000 taels of this bonus into Puyi Bank to increase its working capital. At that time and thereafter, the defendant never used this money for his personal benefit. The defendant admits to withdrawing money from the bank, but this was for public expenses, not salaries. The bank was established in 1917, and the defendant was the initiator and organizer. However, the defendant never received any remuneration from the bank for his efforts in initiating and organizing it, either at that time or at any time before 1932. The defendant was an employee of the bank and was the organizer of the bank's affairs. He worked diligently and carefully for about ten years and received no other remuneration except for the aforementioned 135,000 taels. It is reasonable for the board of directors to reward him with this amount. Now, after a lapse of more than three years, he is suddenly ordered to repay this amount. This is simply unreasonable. At the end of the letter, it is stated that the defendant had told the plaintiff that he would not leave China until all matters were settled, as doing so would be misunderstood. However, the plaintiff filed a petition with the court to prevent the defendant from leaving China. The notice was served just ten minutes before midnight on June 29th. This kind of behavior is crude, oppressive, and violates all the rights of the plaintiff. Therefore, he asks the court to cancel the plaintiff's lawsuit and withdraw the order preventing the defendant from leaving China. The plaintiff should pay the litigation costs. The defendant has the right to take action or be advised to take action against the plaintiff for his unwarranted prevention from leaving China and to demand compensation for losses.

The wording of the responses regarding the Meidong Bank and Puyi Real Estate Company cases is the same as that of the U.S. Feng Bank case. However, the defendant stated that the bonus of 135,000 taels for Meidong Bank was fully refunded in 1933. He did this not because he had any obligation, but because the board of directors of Meidong Bank had passed a resolution accepting it at the time.

Liuhegou Coal Mine Company Continues to Issue 2.5 Million Yuan in Company Bonds: Appoints Yanyeh and Jincheng Banks as Underwriters, Designated for Repaying Small Outstanding Debts 109

Dagong News Agency reports that the Liuhegou Coal Mine Company, whose mining area is located between Hebei and Henan provinces, has extremely thick coal seams. The coal produced is mostly transported to the Yangtze River basin. Last year, due to the accumulation of old debts that urgently needed to be cleared, it issued 1.5 million yuan in company bonds. This year, due to the large amount of outstanding miscellaneous loans, it is continuing to issue 2.5 million yuan, with an annual interest rate of 8%, stipulating that it will be repaid in 11 years. It is understood that these company bonds have been submitted to the Ministry of Industry for detailed review of the issuance regulations and have been entrusted to Yanyeh and Jincheng Banks to underwrite the bonds. As for the underwriting method, it is said that it is completely the same as the underwriting method for the first company bonds, designated for repaying small outstanding debts.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Shanghai-Guangdong Line: Increases Service and Shortens Sailing Time; Designates Yuanheng, Lizhen, and Anxing Ships 111

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's ships driven by Chinese crew members have obtained Hong Kong licenses to sell Hong Kong passenger tickets, and business has increased sharply. It has been decided to shorten sailing times and increase the number of services. The details are as follows:

Obtaining Licenses and Selling Hong Kong Tickets: After the Hong Kong authorities approved the issuance of Hong Kong passenger licenses for ships driven by Chinese crew members, in addition to the original license for the Haiyuan ship, the Haiheng, Haili, and Haizhen ships have all obtained licenses and are selling Hong Kong passenger tickets. These four ships are the newest of the inland ships, with complete equipment. When sailing on the Shanghai-Qingdao line and the Shanghai-Shantou-Hong Kong-Guangdong line, the special and first-class passenger cabins are always fully booked. The fares from Shanghai to Hong Kong are 50 yuan for special class, 24 yuan for first class, 17 yuan for second class, 9.50 yuan for third class, and 7.60 yuan for fourth class. Drinks are not charged extra.

Shortening Sailing Time and Increasing Service: General Manager Liu Hongsheng, to facilitate passengers on the Shanghai-Shantou-Hong Kong-Guangdong line, has decided to shorten the sailing time and increase the number of services. It has now been decided that three ships will sail from Shanghai each week, with the round-trip sailing time shortened to 12 days. The Yuanheng, Lizhen, and Anxing ships will be designated, as well as five other ships, while the Haiyi ship sailing on the Shanghai-Haiphong line will also sell Shantou-Hong Kong-Guangdong passenger tickets. It was originally scheduled to be implemented in August, but due to insufficient preparation, it has been changed to September.

Wu Zhihui, Zhang Xun, Zhang Jingjiang, Ye Gongchuo, Dong Kang, Ding Fubao, Zhang Jiongbo, Yang Kailing, Zheng Jiaxiang, Yu Daxiong, and others, considering that ancient coins in our country, with their long history and exquisite craftsmanship, are not only appreciated by antique enthusiasts day and night, but also have a profound relationship with the world economy and our country's finance, and that people from various countries are vying to study them while we in our own country treat them like worn-out shoes, which is truly lamentable. Bao Feng Steamer at Antou Port - Encountered Storm, Broke Chain, Lost Anchor - Personnel Have Been Dispatched for Salvage 114

The Bao Feng steamer, operated by Jufeng Company on the Chongming-Shanghai route, arrived at Antou Port at 8:25 AM on the 25th of this month. Due to the severe storm, the shipowner, fearing an accident, immediately dropped anchor. However, due to the strong wind and turbulent waters, the anchor chain broke in two sections, and a "God of Immortals" anchor, weighing fifteen hundredweight, also fell into the port. The total value of the anchor and chain was substantial. At that time, the water depth in the port was thirteen feet. Crew members were immediately dispatched to salvage the anchor, working for six and a half hours from 8:30 AM until the tide rose at 3:00 PM, but they were unable to recover it. At 3:15 PM, the Bao Feng steamer sailed back to Shanghai. The shipowner left a second mate in Antou Port to salvage the anchor. Upon the ship's return to Shanghai, the shipowner, Xue Jinlong, reported the incident to the company, which in turn notified the insurance company to send someone to inspect the lost anchor and proceed with the salvage operation.
